# <a id="directory">Directory</a>

## <a id="40-Prado">40 Prado Homeless Services Center</a>

- **Website:** [capslo.org/40-prado](https://capslo.org/40-prado/)
- **Location:** 40 Prado Road, SLO <a href="#" class="map-link" data-lat="35.256218" data-lon="-120.672031" data-zoom="17" data-label="40 Prado Homeless Services Center">Map</a>
- **Phone:**
   - [805-544-4004 x2](tel:+1-805-544-4004;ext=2) (general services) <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/40-prado-warming-center/ -->
   - [805-544-4004 x100](tel:+1-805-544-4004;ext=100) (more information)
   - [805-459-1073](tel:+1-805-459-1073) (questions about on-site safe parking)
- **Hours:** every day, 8am‚Äì2:30pm and 4:30pm‚Äì7am (closed 2:30pm‚Äì4:30pm and 7‚Äì8am) <!-- Though https://capslo.org/40-prado/ says "This facility runs 24/7" -->
   - Overnight shelter intake: M‚ÄìTh 9am‚Äì2pm, Fridays by appointment only <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/40-prado-warming-center/ --> (Intake is a one-time registration process where you provide personal information, complete paperwork, and get added to the shelter system)
   - Laundry services: 8am‚Äì2:30pm
   - Day services: 8am‚Äì4pm <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/safe-parking/ -->
   - Breakfast: before 9am <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/40-prado-warming-center/ -->
   - Lunch: Noon‚Äì12:30pm (open to all) <!-- https://www.slopeopleskitchen.org/serving-info -->
   - Overnight shelter check-in: daily, 4:30‚Äì6pm (Check-in is done each day you want a bed; you must arrive during check-in hours to secure a spot for that night)
   - Dinner: 5‚Äì5:30pm (overnight shelter and cooling center residents only)
   - Warming Center: 7pm‚Äì8am (only when warming center is in operation) <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/40-prado-warming-center/ -->
   - Cooling Center: 8am‚Äì6pm (only when cooling center is in operation) <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/40-prado-warming-center/ -->
   - Safe Parking: 6pm‚Äì7pm <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/safe-parking/ -->
- **How to access:** come to the shelter during intake hours
   - To use the shelter, you must be homeless, you must have a valid photo ID, and you must not have a P.C. 290 sex offender criminal record. You must be able to care for yourself independently (bathing, feeding, dressing, etc.). There are a limited number of beds; priority is given to SLO county residents.
- Notes:
   - operates [**Rotating Overnight Safe Parking Program**](#Rotating-Overnight-Safe-Parking-Program)
   - operates [**SLO Hub**](#SLO-Hub) <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/40-prado/ -->
   - operates the ‚ÄúMid County Warming and Cooling Center‚Äù <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/40-prado-warming-center/ -->
   - operates the ‚Äú40 Prado Safe Parking Program‚Äù <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/safe-parking/ -->
   - [**Healthcare for the Homeless Program**](#HCHP) takes place at 40 Prado
   - [**People‚Äôs Kitchen**](#Peoples-Kitchen-SLO) takes place at 43 Prado <!-- https://www.slopeopleskitchen.org/serving-info -->
   - [**Recuperative Care Program**](#Recuperative-Care-Program) takes place at 40 Prado <!-- Source: https://capslo.org/40-prado/ -->

Grand Ave., Arroyo Grande <a href="#" class="map-link" data-lat="35.118597" data-lon="-120.594462" data-zoom="17" data-label="5Cities Homeless Coalition Warming Center">Map</a> <!-- Source: https://5chc.org/sites/default/files/2024-02/New%20Warming%20Center%20Talking%20Points.pdf -->
- **Phone:**
   - [805-574-1638](tel:+1-805-574-1638) <!-- Source: https://5chc.org/contact-us -->
   - [805-202-3615](tel:+1-805-202-3615) (warming center hotline) <!-- Source: https://5chc.org/programs/warming-center -->
   - [805-295-1501](tel:+1-805-295-1501) (warming center) <!-- Source: https://5chc.org/sites/default/files/2024-02/New%20Warming%20Center%20Talking%20Points.pdf -->
   - [805-295-1501](sms:+1-805-295-1501?&amp;body=Add%20Me) (warming center automatic text updates) <!-- Source: https://5chc.org/programs/warming-center -->
- **Email:** [info@5chc.org](mailto:info@5chc.org) <!-- Source: https://5chc.org/contact-us -->
   - [shelter@5chc.org](mailto:shelter@5chc.org) (warming center) <!-- Source: https://5chc.org/sites/default/files/2024-02/New%20Warming%20Center%20Talking%20Points.pdf -->
- Notes:
   - operates [**Cabins for Change**](#Cabins-for-Change) and ‚ÄúBalay Ko on Barka‚Äù a.k.a. ‚ÄúMy Home for Hope‚Äù
   - operates [**Supportive Services for Veteran Families**](#Supportive-Services-for-Veteran-Families)
   - operates ‚ÄúHomeless Youth Outreach‚Äù
   - hosts the ‚ÄúPet Resource Center‚Äù of [**C.A.R.E.4Paws**](#C.A.R.E.4Paws)
   - entry-point for the [**Coordinated Entry System (CES)**](#CES)

- **How to access:** ‚ÄúImmediate care‚Äù or ‚Äúurgent care‚Äù centers accept walk-ins. Otherwise, make an appointment.
   - Accepts private pay, full- and partially-insured, Medi-Cal, and Medicare. Also offers a sliding fee scale based on income and family size to people without any health insurance. <!-- Source: https://www.communityhealthcenters.org/patient-resources/payment-options-test/ -->
- Notes:
   - Also operates [**Healthcare for the Homeless Program**](#HCHP) at the [**40 Prado Homeless Services Center**](#40-Prado)
   - ‚ÄúCHC Transportation Services‚Äù is a door-to-door ride service to appointments ([877-743-3242](tel:+1-877-743-3242))

- **Locations:**
   - 6370 Atascadero Ave., Atascadero <a href="#" class="map-link" data-lat="35.486312" data-lon="-120.670295" data-zoom="17" data-label="El Camino Homeless Organization">Map</a> <!-- Source: https://www.echoshelter.org/atascadero -->
   - 1134 Black Oak Dr., Paso Robles <a href="#" class="map-link" data-lat="35.645387" data-lon="-120.687569" data-zoom="17" data-label="El Camino Homeless Organization">Map</a> <!-- Source: https://www.echoshelter.org/pasorobles -->
- **Phone:** [805-462-FOOD](tel:+1-805-462-3663) <!-- Source: https://www.echoshelter.org/contact -->
- **Email:** [wlewis@echoshelter.org](mailto:wlewis@echoshelter.org) <!-- Source: https://www.echoshelter.org/contact -->
- **How to access:**
   - For transitional housing, contact ECHO to get on a waiting list; for dinner/showers/laundry, just show up on time
   - Emergency shelter bed signup at the Paso Robles location only, 4:30‚Äì5:30pm <!-- Source: https://www.echoshelter.org/pasorobles -->
- Notes:
   - Dinner (also available to non-residents) at 5pm at both locations <!-- Source: https://www.echoshelter.org/atascadero https://www.echoshelter.org/pasorobles -->
   - Showers (available to non-residents) M‚ÄìF from 4‚Äì5:30pm at both locations <!-- Source: https://www.echoshelter.org/atascadero https://www.echoshelter.org/pasorobles -->
   - Laundry (available to non-residents) W from 10am‚Äì6pm at the Paso Robles location. <!-- Source: https://www.echoshelter.org/pasorobles -->
   - The Paso Robles location operates as an emergency warming center during adverse weather <!-- Source: https://www.echoshelter.org/pasorobles -->

- Medi-Cal Rx:
   - **Website:** [medi-calrx.dhcs.ca.gov](https://medi-calrx.dhcs.ca.gov/)
   - **Phone:** [800-977-2273](tel:+1-800-977-2273)
- Medi-Cal Shuttle: *See [**Ride-On Transportation**](#Ride-On-Transportation)*
- Notes:
   - [**CenCal Health**](#CenCal) is the local Medi-Cal administrator <!-- Source: https://www.slocounty.ca.gov/departments/social-services/medical-resources/services/medi-cal -->
   - Apply at [www.coveredca.com](https://www.coveredca.com/) or [BenefitsCal.com](https://benefitscal.com/) or in person at local DSS offices <!-- Source: https://www.slocounty.ca.gov/departments/social-services/medical-resources/services/medi-cal -->

## <a id="Sunny-Acres">Sunny Acres</a>

‚ÄúSunny Acres‚Äù may refer to two different locations in the city of SLO:

1. a former orphanage in the hills above Johnson Avenue that is now ‚ÄúBishop Street Studios‚Äù operated by [**Transitions Mental Health Association (TMHA)**](#TMHA)
1. a former sober living compound near Laguna Lake that is now the [**Healing and Restoration Campus**](#Healing-and-Restoration-Campus) operated by [**Restorative Partners**](#Restorative-Partners)

## <a id="Urgent-Care">Urgent Care</a>

There are several urgent care options, including:

- [**Community Health Center**](#CHC) (Arroyo Grande)
- [**Carbon Health Urgent Care**](#Carbon-Health-Urgent-Care-Atascadero) (Atascadero)
- [**Dignity Health Urgent Care**](#Dignity-Health-Urgent-Care) (Atascadero)
- [**Urgent Care of Atascadero**](#Urgent-Care-of-Atascadero)
- [**Urgent Care of Morro Bay**](#Urgent-Care-of-Morro-Bay)
- [**Carbon Health Urgent Care**](#Carbon-Health-Urgent-Care-Paso-Robles) (Paso Robles)
- [**Community Health Center**](#CHC) (Paso Robles)
- [**North County Care Minor Emergency Services**](#North-County-Care) (Paso Robles)
- [**Dignity Health Urgent Care**](#Dignity-Health-Urgent-Care) (Pismo Beach)
- [**Urgent Care Pismo Beach**](#Urgent-Care-Pismo-Beach)
- [**Cottage Urgent Care**](#Cottage-Urgent-Care) (SLO)
- [**Family and Industrial Medical Center**](#Family-and-Industrial-Medical-Center) (SLO)
- [**MedStop**](#MedStop) (SLO)
- [**Community Health Center**](#CHC) (Templeton)

- Eligibility: This program is restricted to people for whom both of the following requirements are true:
   - You are pregnant, breastfeeding, gave birth or had a pregnancy loss in the past six months, or you care for a child under the age of five
   - And you live in California and have income below a certain threshold, or receive Medi-Cal, [CalWORKs](#CalWORKs), or CalFresh benefits.
